# <a name="office-365-management-activity-api-schema"></a><span data-ttu-id="1fc74-103">Esquema da API da Atividade de Gerenciamento do Office 365</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-103">Office 365 Management Activity API schema</span></span>
 
<span data-ttu-id="1fc74-104">O esquema da API da Atividade de Gerenciamento do Office 365 é fornecido como um serviço de dados em duas camadas:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-104">The Office 365 Management Activity API schema is provided as a data service in  two layers:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="1fc74-105">**Esquema comum**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-105">**Common schema**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1fc74-106">A interface para acessar os principais conceitos de auditoria do Office 365, como Tipo de Registro, Hora de Criação, Tipo de Usuário e Ação, além de fornecer dimensões principais (como ID de Usuário), detalhes de local (como endereço IP do Cliente) e propriedades específicas do produto (como Identificação do Objeto).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-106">The interface to access core Office 365 auditing concepts such as Record Type, Creation Time, User Type, and Action as well as to provide core dimensions (such as User ID), location specifics (such as Client IP address), and product-specific properties (such as Object ID).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1fc74-107">Ele estabelece exibições uniformes e consistentes para os usuários extraírem todos os dados de auditoria do Office 365 em algumas exibições de nível superior com os parâmetros apropriados e fornece um esquema fixo para todas as fontes de dados, o que reduz significativamente o custo do aprendizado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-107">It establishes consistent and uniform views for users to extract all Office 365 audit data in a few top level views with the appropriate parameters, and provides a fixed schema for all the data sources, which significantly reduces the cost of learning.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1fc74-108">O esquema Comum é originado de dados de produto que pertencem a cada equipe de produto, como o Exchange, o SharePoint, o Azure Active Directory, o Yammer e o OneDrive for Business.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-108">Common schema is sourced from product data that is owned by each product team, such as Exchange, SharePoint, Azure Active Directory, Yammer, and OneDrive for Business.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1fc74-109">O campo Identificação do Objeto pode ser estendido por equipes de produto para adicionar propriedades específicas do produto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-109">The Object ID field can be extended by product teams to add product specific properties.</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="1fc74-110">**Esquema específico do produto**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-110">**Product-specific schema**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1fc74-111">Desenvolvido com base no esquema Comum para fornecer um conjunto de atributos específicos do produto; por exemplo, esquema do Sway, esquema do SharePoint, esquema do OneDrive for Business e esquema de administração do Exchange.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-111">Built on top of the Common schema to provide a set of product-specific attributes; for example, Sway schema, SharePoint schema, OneDrive for Business schema, and Exchange admin schema.</span></span>
    
<span data-ttu-id="1fc74-112">**Qual camada você deve usar para o seu cenário?**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-112">**Which layer should you use for your scenario?**</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="1fc74-113">Em geral, se os dados estiverem disponíveis em uma camada superior, não retorne a uma camada inferior.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-113">In general, if the data is available in a higher layer, don't go back to a lower layer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1fc74-114">Em outras palavras, se os requisitos de dados puderem ser ajustados a um esquema específico do produto, não é preciso retornar ao esquema Comum.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-114">In other words, if the data requirement can be fit in a product-specific schema, you don't need to go back to the Common schema.</span></span> 

## <a name="office-365-management-api-schemas"></a><span data-ttu-id="1fc74-115">Esquemas da API de Gerenciamento do Office 365</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-115">Office 365 Management Activity API</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="1fc74-116">Este artigo fornece detalhes sobre o esquema Comum, bem como cada um dos esquemas específicos de produto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-116">This article provides details on the Common schema as well as each of the product specific schemas.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1fc74-117">A tabela a seguir descreve os esquemas disponíveis.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-117">The following table describes the reports available in the web service.</span></span> 

|<span data-ttu-id="1fc74-118">Nome do esquema</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-118">Name of schema</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="1fc74-119">Descrição</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-119">Description</span></span>|

## <a name="common-schema"></a><span data-ttu-id="1fc74-166">Esquema Comum</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-166">Common schema</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="1fc74-167">**EntityType Name**: AuditRecord</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-167">**EntityType Name**: AuditRecord</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="1fc74-168">Parâmetro</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-168">Parameter</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="1fc74-169">Tipo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-169">Type</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="1fc74-170">Obrigatório?</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-170">Mandatory</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="1fc74-171">Descrição</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-171">Description</span></span>|
|:-----|:-----|:-----|:-----|
|<span data-ttu-id="1fc74-172">Id</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-172">Id</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="1fc74-173">Combination GUIDEdm.Guid</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-173">Combination GUIDEdm.Guid</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="1fc74-174">Sim</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-174">Yes</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="1fc74-175">Identificador exclusivo de um registro de auditoria.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-175">Unique identifier of an audit record.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="1fc74-176">RecordType</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-176">RecordType Property</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="1fc74-177">Self.[AuditLogRecordType](#auditlogrecordtype)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-177">Self.[AuditLogRecordType](#auditlogrecordtype)</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="1fc74-178">Sim</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-178">Yes</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="1fc74-179">O tipo de operação indicado pelo registro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-179">The type of operation indicated by the record.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1fc74-180">Confira a tabela [AuditLogRecordType](#auditlogrecordtype) para obter detalhes sobre os tipos de registros de log de auditoria.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-180">See the [AuditLogRecordType](#auditlogrecordtype) table for details on the types of audit log records.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="1fc74-181">CreationTime</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-181">CreationTime</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="1fc74-182">Edm.Date</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-182">Edm.Date</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="1fc74-183">Sim</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-183">Yes</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="1fc74-184">A data e hora no Tempo Universal Coordenado (UTC) de quando o usuário realizou a atividade.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-184">The date and time in Coordinated Universal Time (UTC) when the user performed the activity.</span></span>|

## <a name="sharepoint-sharing-schema"></a><span data-ttu-id="1fc74-839">Esquema de compartilhamento do SharePoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-839">SharePoint Sharing schema</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="1fc74-840">Os eventos do SharePoint relacionados ao compartilhamento de arquivos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-840">The file share-related SharePoint events.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1fc74-841">Eles são diferentes dos eventos relacionados a arquivos e pastas em que um usuário está realizando uma ação que afeta outro usuário.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-841">They are different from file- and folder-related events in that a user is taking an action that has some effect on another user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1fc74-842">Para obter informações sobre o esquema de compartilhamento do SharePoint, confira [Usar a auditoria de compartilhamento no log de auditoria do Office 365g](https://support.office.com/en-us/article/Use-sharing-auditing-in-the-Office-365-audit-log-50bbf89f-7870-4c2a-ae14-42635e0cfc01?ui=en-US&amp;rs=en-US&amp;ad=US).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-842">For information about the SharePoint Sharing schema, see [Use sharing auditing in the Office 365 audit log](https://support.office.com/en-us/article/Use-sharing-auditing-in-the-Office-365-audit-log-50bbf89f-7870-4c2a-ae14-42635e0cfc01?ui=en-US&amp;rs=en-US&amp;ad=US).</span></span>

## <a name="dlp-schema"></a><span data-ttu-id="1fc74-1488">Esquema DLP</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-1488">DLP schema</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="1fc74-1489">Os eventos de DLP estão disponíveis para o Exchange Online, o SharePoint Online e o OneDrive For Business.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-1489">DLP events are available for Exchange Online, SharePoint Online, and OneDrive For Business.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1fc74-1490">Observe que os eventos de DLP no Exchange só estão disponíveis para eventos com base na política DLP unificada (por exemplo, configurados por meio do Centro de Conformidade e Segurança).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-1490">Note that DLP events in Exchange are only available for events based on unified DLP policy (e.g. configured via Security & Compliance Center).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1fc74-1491">Não há suporte para eventos de DLP com base em Regras de Transporte do Exchange.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-1491">DLP events based on Exchange Transport Rules are not supported.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="1fc74-1492">Os eventos de DLP (Prevenção contra Perda de Dados) sempre terão UserKey = "DlpAgent" no esquema Comum.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-1492">DLP (Data Loss Prevention) events will always have UserKey="DlpAgent" in the common schema.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1fc74-1493">Existem três tipos DlpEvents armazenados como o valor da propriedade Operation do esquema comum:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-1493">There are three types of DlpEvents which which are stored as the value of the Operation property of the common schema:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="1fc74-1494">DlpRuleMatch – indica que uma regra foi correspondida.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-1494">DlpRuleMatch - This indicates a rule was matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1fc74-1495">Esses eventos existem no Exchange, no SharePoint Online e no OneDrive for Business.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-1495">These events exist in both Exchange and SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1fc74-1496">Para o Exchange, inclui informações de falsos positivos e de substituição.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-1496">For Exchange it includes false positive and override information.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1fc74-1497">Para o SharePoint Online e o OneDrive for Business, falsos positivos e as substituições geram eventos separados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-1497">For SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business, false positive and overrides generate separate events.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="1fc74-1498">DlpRuleUndo – existem apenas no SharePoint Online e no OneDrive for Business e indicam que uma ação de política aplicada anteriormente foi "desfeita" – seja por causa de designação de falso positivo/substituição pelo usuário, ou porque o documento não está mais sujeito à política (seja devido a mudança de política ou alteração de conteúdo no documento).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-1498">DlpRuleUndo - These only exist in SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business, and indicate a previously applied policy action has been “undone” – either because of false positive/override designation by user, or because the document is no longer subject to policy (either due to policy change or change to content in doc).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="1fc74-1499">DlpInfo – existem apenas no SharePoint Online e no OneDrive for Business e indicam uma designação de falso positivo, mas nenhuma ação foi "desfeita".</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-1499">DlpInfo - These only exist in SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business and indicate a false positive designation but no action was “undone.”</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="1fc74-1778">Os sinais de alerta incluem:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-1778">Alert signals include:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="1fc74-1779">Todos os alertas gerados baseados nas [Políticas de alerta no Centro de Conformidade e Segurança](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/securitycompliance/alert-policies#default-alert-policies).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-1779">All alerts generated based on [Alert policies in Security & Compliance Center](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/securitycompliance/alert-policies#default-alert-policies).</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="1fc74-1780">Alertas relacionados ao Office 365 gerados no [Office 365 Cloud App Security](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/securitycompliance/office-365-cas-overview) e no [Microsoft Cloud App Security](https://docs.microsoft.com/pt-BR/cloud-app-security/what-is-cloud-app-security).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-1780">Office 365 related alerts generated in [Office 365 Cloud App Security](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/securitycompliance/office-365-cas-overview) and [Microsoft Cloud App Security](https://docs.microsoft.com/pt-BR/cloud-app-security/what-is-cloud-app-security).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="1fc74-1781">O UserId e o UserKey desses eventos são sempre SecurityComplianceAlerts.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-1781">The UserId and UserKey of these events are always SecurityComplianceAlerts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1fc74-1782">Existem dois tipos de sinais de alerta armazenados como o valor da propriedade Operation do esquema comum:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-1782">There are two types of alert signals which are stored as the value of the Operation property of the common schema:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="1fc74-1783">AlertTriggered – um novo alerta é gerado devido a uma correspondência com a política.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-1783">AlertTriggered - A new alert is generated due to a policy match.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="1fc74-1784">AlertEntityGenerated – uma nova entidade é adicionada a um alerta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-1784">AlertEntityGenerated - A new entity is added to an alert.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1fc74-1785">Este evento somente é aplicável aos alertas gerados com base nas Políticas de alerta no Centro de Conformidade e Segurança do Office 365.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-1785">This event is only applicable to alerts generated based on Alert policies in the Office 365 Security & Compliance Center.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1fc74-1786">Cada alerta gerado pode ser associado a um ou vários desses eventos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-1786">Each generated alert can be associated with one or multiple of these events.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1fc74-1787">Por exemplo, uma política de alerta é definida para disparar um alerta se um usuário exclui mais de 100 arquivos em cinco minutos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-1787">For example, an alert policy is defined to trigger an alert if any user deletes more than 100 files in 5 minutes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1fc74-1788">Se dois usuários ultrapassarem o limite ao mesmo tempo, haverá dois eventos AlertEntityGenerated, mas apenas um evento AlertTriggered.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-1788">If two users exceed the threshold around the same time, there will be two AlertEntityGenerated events, but only one AlertTriggered event.</span></span>

## <a name="office-365-advanced-threat-protection-and-threat-intelligence-schema"></a><span data-ttu-id="1fc74-2246">Esquema de Proteção Avançada contra Ameaças e Inteligência contra Ameaças do Office 365</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-2246">Office 365 Advanced Threat Protection and Threat Intelligence schema</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="1fc74-2247">Os eventos de Proteção Avançada contra Ameaças (ATP) e Inteligência contra Ameaças do Office 365 estão disponíveis para clientes do Office 365 que possuem uma assinatura ATP, Inteligência contra Ameaças ou E5.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-2247">Office 365 Advanced Threat Protection (ATP) and Threat Intelligence events are available for Office 365 customers who have an ATP,  Threat Intelligence, or E5 subscription.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1fc74-2248">Cada evento no feed de ATP e da Inteligência contra Ameaças corresponde aos seguintes itens que foram designados para conter uma ameaça:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-2248">Each event in the ATP and Threat Intelligence feed corresponds to the following that were determined to contain a threat:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="1fc74-2249">Detecção em mensagens de email enviadas ou recebidas por um usuário na organização no momento da entrega e na [Limpeza automática zero hora](https://support.office.com/pt-BR/article/Zero-hour-auto-purge-protection-against-spam-and-malware-96deb75f-64e8-4c10-b570-84c99c674e15).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1fc74-2249">An email message sent by or received by a user in the organization with detections are made on messages at delivery time and from [Zero hour auto purge](https://support.office.com/pt-BR/article/Zero-hour-auto-purge-protection-against-spam-and-malware-96deb75f-64e8-4c10-b570-84c99c674e15).</span></span>
